          "bestPlacement": "Use in Prepare & Access as a short potentiation bridge before sprint, COD, jump, or reactive agility work.",

          "whyItGoesHere": "Belongs in prepare_and_access / potentiate_bridge because the drill\u2019s main adaptation is elastic stiffness and foot reactivity. The placement respects the Vortex rule that high-intent speed, COD, and reactive work must stay fresh, while control and tissue-capacity work sit in resilience or capacity rather than being disguised as warm-up conditioning.",

            "teen": "Use the listed dose with submaximal entry speed first; progress to higher intent only when both sides look symmetrical.",
            "adult_beginner": "Start with fewer reps, larger angles only after landing/braking control is consistent, and avoid fatigue-based COD circuits early.",
            "adult_advanced": "Progress with higher approach velocity, sharper angles, external cues, or sport-specific constraints while keeping total contacts capped.",
            "older_adult": "Use low amplitude, slower approach, longer rest, and prioritize balance, foot placement, and pain-free range over speed.",

              "Finish by sticking, braking, or exiting with the first two steps clean and intentional.",
              "Reset fully before the next rep so every attempt is a quality repetition, not conditioning by accident."
